Didi Horn	SkyX · Founder and CEO	Didi has no shortage of expertise in the world of aviation, aerospace, and drones. Serving with the Air Force for nearly a decade (2006-2015), as both a captain and drone pilot, Didi's work in drone operations would give him profound insight into the capabilities of these unmanned systems.Didi could have taken the easy route, with a solidand stable military career, he could have climbed the ranks right on through to a comfortable retirement. But a restless energy drove him to venture beyond the predictable. There was an entrepreneur within - that could sense the massive potential for UAVs in civilian/industrial applications, long before they became a household name."On the military side, there were drones of every shape and size. On the commercial side, there was virtually nothing." he says, "I thought: 'the world needs a system that offers long-range flight, ease of use, small footprint, and safe operations.' So, I traveled the world, attended countless conferences, challenged executives with my burning questions, and ultimately decided the energy market is where we would forge our success. This industry was sorely lacking an efficient and reliable way to monitor pipelines and other long-range assets."SkyX was born of this dream - and Didi's connections with two brilliant individuals: David Vorsin and Liron Shemesh. Working from coffee shops or any other place they could brainstorm and work, the trio produced a prototype and started building the company, grinding for eight months without any salary."It was a period of extreme focus. During this time, I ran 10-15 kilometers every single morning. At the same time, I was running a marathon of belief that this project would thrive, even when others couldn't see it. I think this kind of strong willpower ultimately makes the difference between success and failure."And then, with a solid prototype and a bit of luck, Didi was introduced to a major investor who saw SkyX's potential and shared in its vision.With the resources to jumpstart their dream, Didi and his crew got to the hard work of building a business, starting in a downtown Toronto "office" that was nothing more than a conference room. Since then, SkyX has become the premium provider of aerial data globally. Using a combination of best-in-class aerial systems and AI-driven anomaly detection, SkyX delivers the actionable data and high-impact reports that customers need to make decisions with confidence. Today, the company is comprised of over 35 employees operating out of its Toronto headquarters - containing corporate offices, flight command center, and manufacturing facility - and international offices in the United States and Europe."With several successful deployments in North America, Europe, and Africa, along with a network of strategic international partnerships, SkyX's end-to-end model for gathering advanced aerial data is gaining serious traction across the globe." said Didi "Not only have we made fantastic progress with our target customers in the energy sector, but the high-quality aerial data we're generating is drawing significant interest from other markets with a need to better visualize operations and assets over vast distances."When asked to reflect on the journey up until now, Didi had this to say:"It's never been work. It's my life. And now, there is a team at my side who want to achieve this dream with me. There's nothing more motivating in the world than that. Ankur Handa	OpenAI · Research Scientist	Understanding real world involves recognising objects, their physical locations and different relationships among them. This is a much higher level scene understanding than 3D reconstruction and camera pose, and has relied mainly on supervised training data which is laborious to obtain and consequently limited. In this work, we show howphoto-realistic simulations and computer graphics can provide the necessary data to ameliorate this problem and help us get a better understanding of real world.Ankur obtained his PhD in Prof. Andrew Davison's robotvision lab at Imperial College London on real-time SLAM and camera tracking. He finished his post-doctoral research at the University of Cambridge with Prof. Roberto Cipolla on scene understanding with his work on SceneNet. He then returned to Andrew's lab as a Dyson Research Fellow and continued his work on using simulations to generate data for machine learning to do scene understanding with SceneNet RGB-D. Retrain is a talent-intelligence platform for Enterprises and Governments to seamlessly assess their workforce’s knowledge, qualifications, and skills, using artificial intelligence and machine learning, enabling them to retrain, recruit, andretain workers faster and more accurately than ever before. Retrain's AI models captures skills shifts cycles and predicts the Jobs-of-the-Future, allowing employers to understand better which skills are emerging, evolving and expiring, so they can re-train their workforce effectively while planning outside talent hiring rapidly, all while empowering job-seekers who have been displaced by automation or global crisis to be re-trained and get back into the workforce.Prior to retrain.ai Shay co-founded of Kaltura ( www.kaltura.com ), a leader in video streaming solutions.
